<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DuPont Delivers 3Q 2010 Earnings of $.40 per Share Despite $.13
Pharmaceuticals Decline</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">2010 EPS Guidance Increased on Continued Global
Sales Growth</font></i></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Highlights:</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DuPont&#146;s
third quarter 2010 earnings per share were $.40, compared to $.45 per share in
the prior year, despite a $.13 decline in Pharmaceuticals income related to
patent expirations.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sales
of $7.0 billion grew 17 percent versus the prior year, principally reflecting
14 percent higher volume.&#160; Sales in
emerging markets increased 22 percent.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">All
segments had robust volume increases, with Safety &amp; Protection up 31
percent and Electronics &amp; Communications up 24 percent.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DuPont
made a $500 million voluntary contribution to its principal U.S. pension plan
in September.&#160; The company expects 2010
free cash flow to be about $1.7 billion.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DuPont
increased its full-year 2010 earnings guidance to about $3.10 per share,
excluding significant items.&#160; The company&#146;s
previous guidance was a range of $2.90 to $3.05 per share.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;I am proud of our business
teams&#146; performance this quarter, with segment pre-tax earnings up 33 percent
excluding Pharmaceuticals income.&#160;&#160;
DuPont&#146;s market focus and science-based innovations helped drive
outstanding sales growth, with all business segments and regions
contributing.&#160; Our deep customer
engagement and disciplined execution are gaining traction toward achieving our
long-term growth targets,&#148; said DuPont Chair and CEO Ellen Kullman.&#160; &#147;This quarter&#146;s results were complemented by
ongoing productivity improvements and rigorous cost management that contributed
to profitable growth.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">E. I.
du Pont de Nemours and Company</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Global Consolidated Sales and Net
Income</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2010 consolidated net sales of $7.0 billion were 17
percent higher than the prior year reflecting 14 percent higher volume, 5
percent higher local selling prices, a 1 percent reduction from currency
exchange rates and a 1 percent reduction from portfolio changes. The table
below shows regional sales and variances versus the third quarter 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">*
Europe, Middle East &amp; Africa</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third
quarter 2010 net income attributable to DuPont was $367 million versus $409
million in 2009.&#160; Pharmaceuticals income
was down substantially in the quarter related to patent expirations.&#160; Fourteen percent higher sales volume was
partly offset by selected growth investments in Agriculture &amp; Nutrition and
Safety &amp; Protection and higher pension expense.&#160; Fixed costs were 45 percent of sales,
improving from 49 percent in third quarter 2009.&#160; Fixed cost productivity is tracking ahead of
pace for the full year.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2<a name="PB_2_123720_7056"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="1" width="25%" noshade color="black" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">*&#160;&#160;&#160; Segment sales include transfers</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Segment pre-tax operating income (PTOI) for third quarter 2010 was $763
million compared to third quarter 2009 PTOI of $757 million.&#160; The $6 million PTOI increase reflects higher
segment sales, more than offsetting an expected decline from Pharmaceuticals as
shown in the table below.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

(LOSS)</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_125027_5796"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='4',FILE='C:\JMS\105538\10-19930-1\task4322233\19930-1-mm-01.htm',USER='105538',CD='Oct 26 15:37 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following is a summary of business results for each of the company&#146;s reportable
segments, comparing third quarter 2010 with third quarter 2009, for sales and
PTOI.&#160; All references to selling price
are on a U.S. dollar basis, including the impact of currency.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Agriculture &amp; Nutrition &#151; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter
2010 sales of $1.3 billion were up $27 million, or 2 percent, principally
reflecting 5 percent higher volume, partially offset by Crop Protection
portfolio changes of 3 percent.&#160;
Increased sales primarily reflect technology penetration in the Latin
American seed market and broad-based sales increase of Rynaxypyr</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;insecticide.&#160; Segment PTOI for the third quarter was a loss
of $181 million, compared to a loss of $113 million in the third quarter 2009,
reflecting growth investments and the impact of divested businesses.&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Year-to-date sales were $7.5 billion, up 9 percent
versus the prior year and year-to-date PTOI was $1.5 billion, up 15 percent.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Electronics &amp; Communications &#151; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter
2010 sales of $703 million were up $161 million, or 30 percent, reflecting 24
percent higher volume and 6 percent higher selling prices, primarily
pass-through of metals prices.&#160; Higher
volume was driven by growth in all regions, particularly in Asia Pacific and
Europe, and strong demand across most market segments, particularly in
photovoltaics.&#160; PTOI of $126 million was
up $49 million reflecting significantly higher volume.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Performance
Chemicals &#151; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2010 sales of $1.7 billion were up
$344 million, or 26 percent, reflecting 15 percent higher volume and 12 percent
higher selling prices.&#160; The sales
increase occurred in all regions, especially in North America and Asia Pacific,
and was driven by strong demand across most market segments, particularly for
titanium dioxide, fluoropolymers and industrial chemicals.&#160; PTOI was $292 million, an improvement of $85
million, primarily due to higher volume and selling prices.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Performance
Coatings &#151; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2010 sales of $937 million were up $55
million, or 6 percent, on 5 percent higher volume.&#160; Results reflect continued strengthening in
North American and European heavy duty truck markets, and increased demand in
global automotive markets, most significant in North America.&#160; PTOI was $64 million, up 10 percent from
higher volume.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Performance
Materials &#151; </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Third quarter 2010 sales of $1.6 billion were up
$275 million, or 21 percent, with 19 percent higher volume and a 4 percent
increase in selling prices.&#160; The higher
volume reflects strong demand in automotive, electronic and packaging markets,
with growth in all regions, particularly Asia Pacific.&#160; PTOI was $281 million, an improvement of 22
percent from higher volume and selling prices, partially offset by the absence
of a $24 million benefit from insurance recoveries in the prior year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Safety
&amp; Protection &#151;</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> Third quarter 2010 sales of $871 million were up
$201 million, or 30 percent, primarily due to higher volume.&#160; Growth reflects increased demand for aramid
and nonwoven products due to strengthening in industrial markets, and strong
demand across all regions.&#160; PTOI was $134
million, an improvement of $76 million from higher volume and the absence of a
$26 million asset impairment charge in the prior year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Additional
information is available on the DuPont Investor Center website at
www.dupont.com.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_125047_2897"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Outlook</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:63.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company expects full-year earnings to be about $3.10 per share,
excluding significant items which will include a fourth quarter $.13 per share
loss on the early extinguishment of debt.&#160;
The previous guidance range was $2.90 to $3.05 per share.&#160; The increased outlook reflects strong third
quarter results and </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">expectations for sustained demand in key global markets, continued pricing
momentum and benefits from ongoing productivity.&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The outlook also assumes
Pharmaceuticals full-year pre-tax income will be about $480 million.&#160; The company expects full-year free cash flow
to be about $1.7 billion.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:63.0pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Use of Non-GAAP Measures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Management believes that certain non-GAAP measurements, such as free
cash flow, are meaningful to investors because they provide insight with
respect to ongoing operating results of the company.&#160; Such measurements are not recognized in
accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP) and should not
be viewed as an alternative to GAAP measures of performance.&#160; Reconciliations of non-GAAP measures to GAAP
are provided in schedules C and D.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">DuPont (www.dupont.com)
is a science-based products and services company. Founded in 1802, DuPont puts
science to work by creating sustainable solutions essential to a better, safer,
healthier life for people everywhere. Operating in more than 90 countries,
DuPont offers a wide range of innovative products and services for markets
including agriculture and food; building and construction; communications; and
transportation.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">:&#160; This news release contains forward-looking
statements based on management&#146;s current expectations, estimates and
projections.&#160; All statements that address
expectations or projections about the future, including statements about the

Many factors, including those discussed more fully elsewhere in this

factors include, but are not limited to changes in the laws, regulations,

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second quarter
and year-to-date 2010 included benefits for the adjustment of accrued interest
of $59 ($38 after-tax) in Other income, net and the adjustment of income tax
accruals of $49 associated with settlements of prior year tax contingencies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second quarter
and year-to-date 2009 included a $(340) restructuring charge recorded in
Employee separation / asset related charges, net related to severance and
related benefit costs, asset related charges, and other non-personnel
costs.&#160; Pre-tax amounts by segment
were:&#160; Electronics&nbsp;&amp;
Communications - $(43); Performance Chemicals - $(66); Performance Coatings -
$(65);&#160; Performance Materials - $(110);
Safety&nbsp;&amp; Protection - $(55); and Other - $(1).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second quarter
and year-to-date 2009 included a $75 reduction in estimated costs recorded in
Employee separation / asset related charges, net related to the 2008
restructuring program primarily due to the achievement of work force reductions
through non-severance programs and redeployments.&#160; Pre-tax amounts by segment were:&#160; Agriculture&nbsp;&amp; Nutrition - $(1);
Performance Chemicals - $3; Performance Coatings - $42; Performance Materials -
$28; Safety&nbsp;&amp; Protection - $1; and Other - $2.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Second quarter
and year-to-date 2009 included a $50 benefit in Cost of goods sold and other
operating charges resulting from a reduction of $26 from lower than estimated
inventory and permanent investment write-offs and $24 in insurance recoveries
relating to the damage from Hurricane Ike in 2008.&#160; Total pre-tax amount related to the
Performance Materials segment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 18.7pt;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .95pt;"><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp; Includes

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">E. I. du Pont de Nemours and Company</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Reconciliation of Non-GAAP Measures</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(Dollars in millions, except per share amounts)</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SCHEDULE D (continued)</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exchange Gains/Losses</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The company routinely uses forward exchange contracts to offset its net
exposures, by currency, related to the foreign currency-denominated monetary
assets and liabilities of its operations. The objective of this program is to
maintain an approximately balanced position in foreign currencies in order to
minimize, on an after-tax basis, the effects of exchange rate changes.&#160; The net pre-tax exchange gains and losses are
recorded in Other income, net on the Consolidated Income Statements and are
largely offset by the associated tax impact.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As shown above, the &#147;Total Exchange Gain (Loss)&#148; is the sum of the
&#147;Subsidiary/Affiliate Monetary Position Gain (Loss)&#148; and the &#147;Hedging Program
Gain (Loss).&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Reconciliation of Base Income Tax Rate to Effective
Income Tax Rate</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Base income tax rate is defined as the
effective income tax rate less the effect of exchange gains/losses, as defined
above, and significant items.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
